Biography of a Famous Person

Biography of Einstein (II) 265

— Cong Mu

The teachers at Münich's school knew that Einstein's mathematical talent was outstanding, so when he left Münich for Milan, they gave him a letter of recommendation for university. Although this had no practical value, it cannot be said that it had no spiritual effect on his future. After half a year of free life, because he was at the age of schooling, he had to go back to school again. However, the language level of Italian schools was very high, and his language skills were very ordinary, making it difficult to get in, so he had no choice but to go to Switzerland. As a result, after some twists and turns, through the introduction of Mr. Earl Alak, the president of the Polytechnic University, he became an upper-level student in science at the Aargau cantonal school in Switzerland, which was in the autumn of 1895.

The atmosphere at Aargau school was very free and open. The education method was different from that of general middle schools, and it was completely in the style of a university. So he was very happy here, as he was in Italy, and made many friends.

Einstein lived in the home of one of his school's liberal arts teachers named Winteler. This teacher had a boy and a girl, who were both very friendly with Einstein and often traveled with him to various parts of Switzerland. Later, the teacher's son married his sister, Maya.

A year later, he easily obtained a certificate and formally became a student of the Polytechnic.

At that time, the professors at the Polytechnic included Weber in physics and Minkowski in mathematics. Weber was the builder of the new mathematics and physics classroom here and was working hard on various experimental studies. Minkowski made very important contributions to Einstein's theory of relativity; at the same time, Professor Kessel's geometry lecture notes also greatly helped the development of the general theory of relativity in the future. However, at this time, Einstein had almost lost interest in mathematics and preferred physics by comparison. In addition to this, he also dabbled in other academic books. At this time, what he loved to read most was Darwin's biology and Mach's philosophical books.

The person closest to him among his classmates was Marcel Grossmann. This person was his collaborator in the development of the general theory of relativity in the future, and his achievements were greatly related to it.

In his second year at the Polytechnic, in 1897, when he was only seventeen years old, Einstein worked hard to study the problems related to light, ether, and the Earth's motion, which were the central problems of the later theory of relativity.

His tuition fees while studying in Switzerland were not paid by his parents, but were given to him by his relatives at one hundred francs per month. In order to obtain Swiss citizenship, he saved twenty francs from it every month, and used the remaining eighty francs to handle all matters. So his life at that time was very poor, and he was malnourished, so that he often suffered from gastrointestinal diseases later.

During his four years of student life in Switzerland, his knowledge was also quite profound. But driven by the idea of truly reaching the core of the natural way, he went on to study philosophy. At that time, he liked to read the works of Kant, Schopenhauer, and Hume, especially inclined towards Hume.

(II)

In the autumn of 1900, when Einstein was twenty-two years old, he graduated from Kiliqi's Polytechnic (equivalent to China's engineering university or polytechnic university), and passed the national examination with excellent grades. His diploma could be used as an official license for mathematics and physics teachers. From then on, he had to leave the help of his uncles and seek his own livelihood, but when he first went to his professors to seek a career, he did not get any results, which can be said to be his first failure to seek a career.

Originally, to be a formal teacher in a Swiss school, one must have Swiss citizenship, but Einstein had not yet obtained it; moreover, he was Jewish, and even in free Switzerland, Jews were everywhere subject to exclusion and oppression. Therefore, it was very difficult for Einstein to find a job after graduating, and he had to taste the pain of unemployment for a while. It wasn't until the second year, 1901, that he found a temporary position at a vocational school. But this position was only temporary after all, so after a few months he was unemployed again and had to temporarily live by relying on friends. Later, he discovered an advertisement in the newspaper asking to hire a home tutor, and after a series of procedures, he finally managed to save a home tutor position.

Most graduates of university physics departments work as technicians or teachers. But after Einstein graduated, he spent a whole year without finding a more suitable position. This was of course a very anxious problem for him. Later, fortunately, his friend from his student days, Marcel Grossmann, sympathized with his poverty and asked his father to write a sincere letter of introduction for Einstein, introducing him to the Director of the Patent Office in Bern, Halla. From this, Einstein began to serve in the Bern Patent Office in 1902. Before this, he had already obtained Swiss citizenship.

After Einstein entered the Patent Office, his life was considered relatively stable. Here, he wanted to make as much use as possible of his spare time and even working time to engage in his great research. However, the regulations of the bureau were that personal matters were not allowed during office hours, so it was really very difficult for Einstein to do his research work during office hours. Sometimes, just as he was drawing a diagram or calculating something on a small piece of paper, if he heard footsteps outside the door, he would immediately stuff the small piece of paper or the diagram he was drawing into the drawer, otherwise, if the director saw it, he would definitely be severely criticized. (To be continued)

Storytelling 268

Yao Xiao'an, Wang Pingqiu, Qilin Leopard

Zhongxi (1040) 8:00 PM to 8:45 PM

Opening Chapter "Winter"

Heavy snow is falling again this winter. Six-petaled flowers fly, heralding a year of abundance. Dark clouds thickly cover the severe cold. Only when winter arrives does snow come again. Only to see every household closing its doors, the streets silent. Only because the cold air does not melt. Like a blade blowing, the skin wants to crack. A mad roar rises from the fence in the bitter wind. The cold is so unusually strong. The curtains outside the window are layered. Still, they report fighting each other. The whole body shivers, and the back bends like a bow. Lowering the head and exhaling into the hands is a poor sight. Bending the back and calling out to the waist is like bowing. Rich families have everything prepared. The poor have no money and are cold and dazed. The wealthy light a roaring fire. The family gathers warmly. It is a pity that at this time, a poor man runs. Running on the snowy road to earn stinky copper. Helplessly braving the cold air. The whole body trembles from the cold attack. In the snow-covered streets, one must work hard. Running around can avoid hunger. Not like wealthy children. Sitting safely in the hall like a great lord. A hundred responses with one call, there is no need to say. Winter snow has nothing to do with the cold air impact. He is unaware of seeking plum blossoms in the snow. Completely mercenary and petty. On weekdays at home, he only flatters. Most in line with his wishes and secretly happy. The winter air condenses cold, startling guests. No door to ask for help, following a vagrant's trail. It is a pity that this man will freeze to death. Who pities and provides food and clothing. Don't say the young master's intention. There is absolutely no kindness in his heart. Even claiming to be a chivalrous hero. It's just a false name, angling with extreme skill. In reality, he does hidden good deeds. He pretends to be stupid like a deaf-mute. A rich man's feast is the millet of a thousand homes. It is truly a sigh to look up at the sky. The path of the world is rough and impassable.

"Orchid in the Empty Valley"

"Good Son"

The mother wants to gamble, the wife wants to dress up, the brothers want pocket money, the landlord wants rent money, and the rice store wants rice money. They don't care about their own son, husband, older brother cannot earn money, and the old lady has money and refuses to take it out. Shen Bao Local Supplement - Film Special

Who is Hollywood's Highest-Earning Star? (Part 2) Chen Xiong 272

On the list of million-dollar films, music productions account for the most, and since the beginning of film history, the dance-song film "Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse" and "Ben-Hur" have consistently held the record for box office revenue in cinemas around the world. With the advent of sound film, "What Price Glory" (also known as "Magnificent Flirt") broke all records, and this film also belongs to the music production category.

Novel productions have a significant impact on box office revenue. Among Janet Gaynor's seven million-dollar productions, "Seventh Heaven" had the highest record with three million. Although this film cannot be considered Janet Gaynor's best work, because she sang for the first time in this film, she used the novelty psychology to attract many viewers.

Although Greta Garbo is a very popular star in Hollywood, her value is several times higher than other stars, but only two of her films have earned over one million U.S. dollars. One is "Anna Christie," her first talkie, because advertisements heavily promoted the novelty of "Garbo talks!" to lure Garbo fans. As expected, "Anna Christie" was three times more profitable, even Garbo could not have imagined it. As for the second million-dollar production, "Grand Hotel," this cannot be considered her personal victory, because the actors in "Grand Hotel," such as the Barrymore brothers, Wallace Beery, Joan Crawford, etc., are all MGM mainstays, and they can at least attract a portion of the revenue.

In the entire list of million-dollar films, we can find a very obvious principle: that in many profitable productions, films with light and cheerful themes account for a large proportion. The endings of these films are usually "lovers become husband and wife" or similar. Although there are a few blockbusters, such as "All Quiet on the Western Front" and "The Birth of a Nation," that end with death.

There was a period when American films were very popular with productions based on gangster bosses. Although they could cause a sensation during public screenings, none of them earned over a million dollars. Therefore, viewers have good judgment when choosing films. Productions that guide society, influence people's hearts, and integrate education with entertainment are welcomed by viewers. Conversely, plots that are shallow and films that copy previous successful productions are rejected by viewers.

Now, we will list some of the important million-dollar films published in the American film industry annual that have been screened in this country:

"What Price Glory" earned five million U.S. dollars, starring Al Jolson, the highest-grossing talkie production.

"The Four Horsemen of the Apocalypse" earned four and a half million, starring the late heartthrob Rudolph Valentino.

"Ben-Hur" earned four million. This film is still popular and being screened, and future revenue will be more than this.

"State Fair," "Sunny Side Up," "Street Angel," "The Winning of Barbara Worth," "The Jazz Singer" 丨丨 Three and a half million.

"Seventh Heaven," "The Man Who Came Back," "Tess of the Storm Country," "Angel," "Delicious," "The Gay Retreat," and "The Man Who Came Back" 丨丨 are all Janet Gaynor's productions. Six of them have been screened in China. The seventh, "The Man Who Came Back," has not been to China because its content involves the face of the Chinese people. The above seven have all earned over one million U.S. dollars, the most being three million three hundred thousand, and the least being one million three hundred thousand. "The Big Parade" 丨 Two million seven hundred thousand. "The Gold Rush," "The Kid," "The Ten Commandments" 丨丨 Two million five hundred thousand.

"42nd Street," "Grand Hotel," "Gold Diggers of Broadway," "Red Dust," "Little Women" 丨丨 Two million two hundred and fifty thousand

"Cimarron," "Resurrection," "Liliom," "Skippy," "The Cock-Eyed World" 丨丨 Two million. "Springtime in the Rockies," "Bad Girl," "All Quiet on the Western Front," "The King of Kings," "City Lights," "Four Sons," "The Hunchback of Notre Dame" 丨丨 One million five hundred thousand or more. (The End)

New Developments in the Hollywood Film Industry in the Past Year 273

— Huang Yingdai

The wheel of time is advancing rapidly, sending away 1934 and welcoming 1935. In the past year, if we review the Hollywood film industry, then besides the fact that American films have special capital colors and occupy special markets in overseas countries, still maintaining the past situation, we can find several new developments:

A Major Shackles First, Hollywood film companies have not had the freedom to make films in the past year as they did before. The so-called cleaning movement has given the American film industry a major shackle. The content of the films, so-called sensuality, and immorality, are all prohibited. In addition, the review board's review regulations are particularly strict, and religious organizations oppose it. When making a film, one must take care not to be sanctioned by one aspect, and also take care not to be opposed by another. It is really a so-called careful and considerate approach in every way, otherwise one will encounter accidents!

The Popularity of Literary Films Under this environment, film companies have taken a new approach of adopting literary works in terms of film production and themes in order to avoid censorship and sanctions. Putting already famous literary works on the screen will naturally not violate the cleaning movement, and will not violate religion. Moreover, because the story has already been read by the general public, and those authors are all admired literary figures, the box office will definitely be very good when the film is released. As evidenced by the fact that in the most recent year, a series of literary films such as "Little Women," "A Bill of Divorcement," "The Count of Monte Cristo," "Treasure Island," etc., had excellent box office when they were released in Shanghai. In addition, historical films are also very popular. Historical themes and literary works are of course equally unrestricted themes. This is a new way out that Hollywood film companies have recently discovered.

Child Stars Having Great Luck Speaking of actors, in 1934, there was a new trend in Hollywood, that is, the stars who were most popular in the film industry were not the generally established movie stars, but several child stars who were just starting out. In the past year, established male and female stars, with the exception of a few, have not made any new achievements or new progress. Strictly speaking, some have even regressed. However, among child stars, such as Shirley Temple's fame in Hollywood, she is already a famous child star. In addition, there are many more child stars who have already appeared on the screen and have the hope of success. Therefore, in Hollywood in 1934, we can call it the year of the full bloom of child stars. Such activity of child stars on the screen may have created a new record in the history of Hollywood films. Parents who are currently experiencing unemployment panic are registering their children with film companies, hoping that their children will become famous child stars and be able to have a wealthy income like Shirley Temple's parents by relying on their daughter's fame!

Film Fans Pay Attention to "Orchid in the Empty Valley" 274

"Orchid in the Empty Valley" was originally a famous silent film of the Star Film Company in those years. The actors at that time included Zhang Zhiyun, Yang Naimei, Zhu Fei, and Zheng Xiaoqiu. Because the plot was tortuous, sad, and moving, it was warmly welcomed by thousands of viewers. When the film was released in various ports last summer, the box office was still strong, from which we can know the immortal value of the film.

In order to meet the needs of people in society, this time, the Star Film Company has changed it into a sound film, still directed by Zhang Shichuan, and starring Hu Die, Gao Zhanfei, Xuan Jinglin, Yan Yuexian, etc. Moreover, this time, many emotions are expressed through dialogue. Of course, sound films are more spectacular than silent films.

It is said that the Star Film Company has recently received an average of at least one hundred letters a day from people from all over asking about the film's news, from which one can predict the grand occasion when the film is released.

About the Soviet Union International Film Festival 275

The Central Propaganda Department Telegraphed the Star Film Company

Inviting Representatives to Beijing to Discuss

The Soviet Union will hold an international film exhibition in February of this year. Ge Gongzhen telegraphed Mr. Zhou Jianyun, manager of the Star Film Company, requesting that the company send representatives and invite representatives from the Lianhua Company, along with Ms. Hu Die, to attend and participate, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now heard that the Central Propaganda Department yesterday telegraphed the Star Film Company again, saying: "According to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' notification that the Soviet Union is preparing to hold a world film exhibition, it is proposed to solicit films from your company and invite famous actors to participate. This matter concerns international dignity. How to respond to the solicitation, it is hoped that you will send personnel to Beijing to discuss the matter in person. Respectfully, the Central Propaganda Department."

"Femme Fatale" Will Be Released Soon 276

After a very long production time and publicity time, and at a huge cost, "Femme Fatale" is a Lianhua blockbuster that the Chinese people are extremely eager to see.

If we say that this film is the most brilliant work among domestic films in recent years, then that is not an exaggeration, because many people have already said this during the first trial screening at the beginning of its completion.

Of course, we can guarantee that this is a masterpiece with amazing progress by Yang Xiaozhong after "Good Night." However, everyone should also know that this film has been able to achieve such success not by accident or luck, but by the hard work, efforts, and a solid spirit of cooperation of the workers.

If you don't believe it, wait and see, this film will be released soon. The entire film, no matter in any aspect, can show its strong posture everywhere. Especially the performances of Chen Yanyan, Zhang Yi, and Liang Saizhen, it should be said that they are so good that nothing can be added.

Film Novel

The Legend of the Red Sheep Hero (6) 278

— Zhao Chu

Hong Xiuquan hurriedly stepped forward, grasped Shi Dakai's hand, turned his face back, and said to Yang and Zeng, "Mr. Shi is both talented in literature and martial arts, and is indeed one of us," he said. Yang and Zeng hurriedly stepped forward to greet him and invited him to sit down. They all sat down by the table. Hong said, "Mr. Shi's esteemed arrival here must be for some insightful advice!" Shi Dakai then said, "I have heard of your actions here and have come specifically to join your ranks, to serve as a humble soldier." Hong joyfully clasped his hands and said, "Mr. Shi's talent and strategy surpasses ours tenfold. This is truly Heaven helping us to overthrow the Qing Dynasty." Shi Dakai then modestly said, "Now that the society members are already so developed, how much preparation is there for military supplies and provisions? According to Mr. Zeng's wealth, it is certainly sufficient to maintain things at present, but if we raise an uprising in the future and there is no support, I fear we will find it difficult. My coming here is firstly to donate my own small estate to the society, and secondly to introduce someone who is capable of being a treasury, to strengthen the society's momentum." Hong, Yang, and Zeng all listened and hurriedly said, "This is truly Mr. Shi's generosity and righteousness, but we do not know who you are referring to?" Shi deliberately smiled and said, "This person is right before our eyes, it is Wei Changhui of Guiping County." Zeng listened and suddenly stood up, excitedly saying, "If Mr. Shi hadn't mentioned it, I would have forgotten. This person is truly an extraordinary figure, with millions in wealth, he is the richest household in this county. But how can we persuade him to join us here?" Shi listened and immediately stood up, saying, "I have some dealings with him. I am willing to persuade him to join us." At that time, Hong, Yang, and Zeng were all very happy and thanked Shi. Suddenly, Xiao Chaogui ran in from outside and said, "Mr. Feng has returned, and Mr. Hong's family members have also been brought along." As he spoke, everyone stood up and went outside to welcome them. Feng Yunshan came in from outside, leading Lai Shi, Hong Xuanjiao, and Feng's wife, all walking in from the courtyard, along with several strong men carrying boxes, luggage, and clothes. Hong spoke some words of consolation to Feng, and Hong Xuanjiao and Lai Shi also came to say words of long absence to Hong. Then they were invited to go into the inner room together.

In the square, Xiao Chaogui was teaching several people how to wield a single broadsword. Xiao himself also performed a set of moves, which were very impressive. The onlookers all clapped their hands and cheered. Xuanjiao, along with a female servant, stood under a tree watching, and couldn't help but shout a cheer. Xiao, in the midst of his enthusiastic sword dance, heard Xuanjiao's cheering and hurriedly stopped his sword, turned around and saw Xuanjiao, and quickly bowed. He walked to her side and said, "I heard that Miss Hong has good martial arts skills. Today, I am bold enough to ask for your guidance." Xuanjiao listened and said with a shy look, "I have learned a few moves, but they are not presentable, I dare not show off." Xiao still pleaded earnestly, and Xuanjiao couldn't refuse, so she took the sword, said "Excuse me," and walked over, performing with the sword, which was very exquisite. The onlookers, warriors, watched and cheered, and Xiao Chaogui was even more mesmerized. When the dance stopped, she ran shyly to Xiao's front, and Xiao praised her vigorously, saying, "Miss Hong's martial arts are truly brilliant! I admire, I admire." Miss Hong shook her head without saying a word, returned the sword to Xiao, and ran away. Hong Xiuquan was talking to Zeng Yuheng when Hong Xuanjiao ran over and said to Xiuquan, "Brother! I want to train a team of female soldiers, which may be useful in the future." Hong and Zeng immediately replied, "This is a very good idea, we can gather them together." Xuanjiao expressed a very happy look and said, "It's even harder to bear being unoccupied with nothing to do."

From then on, Xiao Chaogui became listless and changed his usual state. One day, he used the tip of a sword to draw a crooked, uneven Hong character on the ground, and also wrote a small word, lost in thought. Suddenly, someone secretly came up and patted him on the shoulder, saying, "Brother Xiao! What are you thinking about?" Xiao was startled, looked up, and hurriedly erased the handwriting on the ground, then stood up. It was Qin Rigang standing there laughing. Xiao smiled and replied, "I wasn't thinking about anything, I was thinking about how I could practice my martial arts better." Qin didn't believe his words, but laughed loudly, and Xiao also laughed. However, this was also a matter of marriage. Later, Qin Rigang and Feng Yunshan actually spoke to Hong Xiuquan, and Xuanjiao was betrothed to Xiao Chaogui. (To be continued)
